# Next Critical Images - 2026-06-14 - Next 1000

Generated from current repo asset coverage. Existing files and all destinations already listed in previous image-generation CSV packs were skipped, including the full June 13 next-400 pack.

Language rule: reuse the canonical English/app image across translated copies by default. Only create a separate localized image when the graphic itself has visible language text or the localized page is meaningfully different.

Avatar rule: reference URLs are kept in CSV notes only. The prompt asks for a supplied reference image instead of asking ChatGPT to browse URLs.

Format rule: every row in this pack targets WebP.
